Design — Out Loud App\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/uiux-design-out-loud-app\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/outloud_abdz.png\" width=\"2800\" height=\"1800\" alt=\"UI/UX Design — Out Loud App\" title=\"UI/UX Design — Out Loud App\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>11.25.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/kasilin\">Valery Kasilin</a> is a UI/UX designer based in Moscow, Russian Federation. He shared via his <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/kasilin\">Behance</a> profile, an app design that is a very fitting application for the times we are currently living in. The holidays are coming soon and not everyone has the luxury to spend time with their relatives. Some of the reasons are components of the current life situation or others are purely taken by safety and precautions. These situations can definitely add uncertainties to your mental health that is already complicated nor hard to deal with during the past months. Valery's concept is an app called: 'Out Loud', it's a mobile application for those who are going through difficult times and can't share with anyone. Even though, it's a personal experiment. I love the fact that Valery tackle a problem is becoming a reality and has been affecting every single of us, I applaud this concept.</p>\n\n<h3>Links</h3>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/kasilin\">https://www.behance.net/kasilin</a></li>\n</ul><p style=\"line-height:1.38\"><img src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/0iQg1lWmFYWVrwSKnBeDfyxweCawI0aIGDa_u7Z341DYoPfBh6Rcp3uIUnveUhxkR8uAKERIO5E2Mk6t6D6fZG974Bk17nBlpe8Qe1ufcv5CmFN8rMSlxDsCfzhBAbb8bNUThNdk\" /></p>\n\n<p><img alt=\"Image may contain: screenshot, letter and abstract\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/8thvlo92DGJe7TQn-st12eNtdf6cZOAbpTph3ydaP3t72oSDwPw-rXUft9UpFuhV0e7lzkBCpdKm_uEAwMk3tshIP8mvZpumc7Wm-fcxPM7aq0wpa2QV4Cq9A9EF_9kSOz6TfLDt\" /></p>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/FnGHmY8KDzsF9e3ZVKY4DZio-TwjzJtB7Z0yifMrFxrMWZ4qwUe9Y-xrIcL0qyqIL7aah2PPdAPkJHz0DBIyoPhbqQKJ_Hdsuxu3Pl-sF8invH2AGdsM8T-d7_R-pJQPkRQVo7uH\" /></p>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://vimeo.com/476963026\">\n<div style=\"max-width:1440px;margin:auto;\"><!-- You're using demo endpoint of Iframely API commercially. Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/remarkable-2-packaging-design-goods\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_reMarkable.jpg\" width=\"1400\" height=\"875\" alt=\"reMarkable 2 Packaging Design by Goods\" title=\"reMarkable 2 Packaging Design by Goods\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>11.25.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p style=\"line-height:1.38\">In close collaboration with the design team at <a href=\"https://remarkable.com/\">reMarkable</a>, Norwegian packaging studio <a href=\"https://goods.no/\">Goods</a> has designed a range of packaging for reMarkable 2. The recently launched device is the world’s thinnest tablet — it's only 4.7mm thick, and aims to replace your notes and printed documents with a digital notebook that feels like paper. The device is designed to be free from distractions and does not feature notifications, social media or email.</p>\n\n<p>To clearly communicate the product, its packaging is used as a canvas to emboss product silhouette at 1:1 scale for a tangible and tactile experience. All packages are recyclable worldwide as paper and features a custom-molded pulp as a device tray. Instead of industry-standard plastic film, the paper tablet comes wrapped in a bespoke, die-cut translucent paper.</p>\n\n<p>The new packaging is half the size of the previous version, which not only reduces both material use and production cost — but also doubles shipping density. The packaging follows a modular sizing system to further support shipping as little air as possible.</p>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\"><img lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>11.29.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>New week, a new abdz. 'Raw Design Inspiration' to kick it off. No theme, absolutely 'raw' inspiration. Being an abdz., inspiration is one of the biggest fuels in my everyday life. Whatever it is for life and work balance, it comes in many shapes and forms. For me, I do appreciate a good surf on <a href=\"https://dribbble.com/\">Dribbble</a>. It's all about how we consume our feeds, I noticed a shift of change from designers on sharing their work on social media platforms like Instagram. I might be an old-timer but I am not too keen on sharing work for likes and shares, I do enjoy the good 'old' Dribbble. It's always gratifying and you usually do find something to spark your mind and inspiration.</p>\n\n<p>The concept of 'Raw' is to randomize what inspires me to kick off my week, maybe it could have the same effect on you. This is reasonably an homage to abdz. daily inspiration series. It's an experiment, and we’ll see how it goes. If you do have a suggestion, you can <a href=\"https://docs.google.com/document/d/1Pg0aEsRlgNLVucn2TyJ2TAI-eDEKBe-8SnJJnSgk_Is/edit?usp=sharing\">submit your work</a>.</p>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/Ce9hm3VP9M6XxHqKPUH-w3Dhn8pMVTagsecF8uWpsp5n46Dh44TXRTwJenouofpIz8jpWxaCl9iFRuBhMCjOpMU3lSy7XLAhITefkzDiWYXfcsf8vREtjSo-lujgK7l3DlM9USWT\" /></p>\n\n<h5>By <a href=\"https://dribbble.com/galshir\">Gal Shir</a></h5>\n\n<div data-oembed-url=\"https://dribbble.com/shots/14667792-Orange-Juice\">\n<div style=\"max-width:1440px;margin:auto;\"><!-- You're using demo endpoint of Iframely API commercially. is an art director based in Mumbai, India. He shared a cool 3D project via his <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/KaranGujar\">Behance</a>. Inspired by human body shapes, he explored the outlines of 3D, shapes, and lighting to come up with this lovely series titled: 'Contour - Scapes'. I love the subtle gradient fading in the background and its repetition. It makes you really focus on the 'waves', I can't help to notice this series totally reminds you of some of the opening titles from these famous 'James Bond' movies. What do you think?</p>\n\n<h3>Links</h3>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/KaranGujar\">https://www.behance.net/KaranGujar</a></li>\n\t<li><a Identity","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/JBEiYmTxNdI/mostra-de-arte-da-juventude-branding-and-visual-identity","description":"Mostra de Arte da Juventude Branding and Visual Identity\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/mostra-de-arte-da-juventude-branding-and-visual-identity\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_sesc.jpg\" width=\"1920\" height=\"1280\" alt=\"Mostra de Arte da Juventude Branding and Visual Identity\" title=\"Mostra de Arte da Juventude Branding and Visual Identity\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>11.24.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p style=\"line-height:1.38\">In 2019, the MAJ (Youth Art Exhibition) celebrated its 30th anniversary and Sesc invited <a href=\"https://polar.ltda/\">Polar</a> to develop the project’s new logo, as well as the branding, visual identity, and signage of the commemorative edition. Following the format of traditional art salons, the exhibition sheds light on contemporary young art production. Currently, it is one of the main cultural events in the interior of the state of São Paulo and places the city of Ribeirão Preto on the Brazilian’s visual arts map.</p>\n\n<p>The new MAJ logo was designed combining geometric shapes with ink traps that pushes it away from a typically modernist solution. The highlight is the character ‘M’, which gains an extra “leg” to reproduce the boost given to MAJ’s featured artists.</p>\n\n<p>The 30-year edition’s visual identity simultaneously pays tribute to the new artists discovered and the city of Ribeirão Preto. We created a series of graphics that refer to sparks, representing young talents at the time of expansion and professional growth, as well as Ribeirão ‘s powerful sun.</p>\n\n<div
